湊斗景明が言った事は、本来なら大鳥香奈枝の言うべき事であり、実際に言ってもいる事なのだ。　彼が困惑したのは無理もない。
What Minato Kageaki had said was what Ootori Kanae should have said, and what she actually said.　It was no wonder he was confused.

幸運があと一ミリグラムほど不足していたら、彼女は今頃地上の存在ではなくなっていただろう。　復讐者が仇敵の命を自らの命で購ったことになる。

大鳥香奈枝は流血を好み殺人を好む。　貴種たる誇り、正義への志向と共存して、その嗜好はあった。
Ootori Kanae loved bloodshed and preferred killing.　This preference coexisted with her pride in her noble breed and her desire for justice.

だから彼女は戦場へ立つ。　貴族たる自分、正道を行く自分、殺人鬼たる自分を揺らがせず全て充たすために。
That's why she stands on the battlefield.　In order to satisfy all of her noble self, her righteous self, and her murderous self without wavering.

わけても復讐は最良の戦場だ。　奪われた嘆きにかけて奪い返す――この正義に疑いを挟む余地はない。
Revenge, in particular, is the best battlefield.　There is no room for doubt about the justice of taking back what was taken from you.

彼女は過去、幾つもの復讐を代行した。　法の担い手、貴族としての責務を全うした。　　その過程に快楽した。

The cause of the disorder was not so much heat exhaustion as it was discrepancies in bodily functions.　The former could not be recovered without sufficient rest, while the latter could be recovered only by calming down the disturbed body and mind.

短い戦闘離脱時間を使い、俺はそれに成功していた。
Using the short time off from combat, I had succeeded in doing just that.

武者の生命線である熱量の運用について、余りにも配慮がない。　終始、全開。
There is no consideration for the operation of heat, which is the lifeline of musha.　Full throttle from start to finish.

態勢を立て直した村正は、敵騎の猛進に付き合う愚を戒め、勢いを受け流し、凌ぎ切る戦いに徹した。　その戦術の効果が顕れるまで、大して長い時間ではなかったろう。
Having regained his bearings, Muramasa refrained from the folly of keeping up with the onslaught of the enemy craft, and concentrated on fighting to pass the momentum and outlast it.　It would not be long before the effects of his tactics became apparent.

四倍の熱量とて、無分別に放出すれば忽ち尽く。　累代の財産がたった一人の浪費家に使い潰されるのと同じ事だ。
Four times the amount of heat, if released carelessly, will quickly run out.　It's as if the wealth of generations is being used up by a single wasteful person.

「先刻は丸腰だったから譲ったまで。　二度は許さん。貴様の目的が殿下であろうと花枝様であろうと果たさせん。俺の前から去りたくば、屍になって黄泉路をゆけ！」
"You were unarmed last time, so I gave you up.　I will not allow you to do it again. I won't allow you to do it again, no matter whether your goal is His Highness or Hanae-sama. If you wish to leave my presence, become a corpse and travel the path of Hades!

".......

こうなっては問答を続けるだけ時間の無駄。　俺は心胆を据え直し、武者として勝負に応ずるべく構えた。
In this situation, it's a waste of time to keep asking and answering.　I regained my composure and prepared to play the game as a musha.

「篠川中将ともあろう者が、己を一介の武者となし太刀打される存念とは。　匹夫の勇と申し上げたいが致し方なし」
I wish I could say that I am a brave man, but I cannot.　I would like to say that I am a man of courage, but I cannot help it.

What is the name of your craft?

"You can't name a weapon.

It became a figure of Sangami-dan.　Both sides put the enemy's shadow within the range of the slash down.

大鳥獅子吼の上段はやや刃先が高い。　太刀を寝かせ気味のこちらに比して、刃尺を明らかにする不利を負う一方、斬撃の到達時間は短縮される。
The upper part of the Ootori Shishiku has a slightly higher blade tip.　While it has the disadvantage of revealing the length of the blade compared to this sword, which is laid down, the arrival time of the slash is shortened.

斯様な構を使うからには、獰猛にすぐさま打ち込んで来る肚かと思いきや、　　――来ない。
I was expecting him to use such a structure and immediately strike with ferocity, but he did not.

沈静である。　野原にぽつり、孤独に佇む枯れ木の風情をもって、大鳥獅子吼は止している。
It is serene.　Ootori Shishiku has the appearance of a dead tree standing alone in a field.

（激情と鋭気のみの男に思われたが）
He seemed to be a man of only passion and sharpness.

俺は対手への評価を修正する必要に迫られた。　敵を呑んで掛かる意気に満ちて剛剣を扱う、戦場の猛将ではなく――むしろ剣術使いの心技を備えていると見られる。
I had to revise my assessment of my opponent.　He is not a fierce general on the battlefield, handling a rigid sword with a gusto that swallows his enemies - rather, he is seen as having the mind and skills of a swordsman.

それが彼本来の剣質なのかどうかは置き、今この場の争闘において適性である事は認めねばならなかった。　地上、しかも狭隘な屋内である。
Whether or not this was his natural sword quality, he had to admit that it was suitable for the current struggle.　It was on the ground, and in a narrow room.

天空を翔ける翼はおろか、金剛力も充分には発揮し難い。力と速度を恃む武者刀法が特に苦手とする局面であった。　このような場では精妙な術技こそが物を言う。
It's hard to use your wings to fly in the sky, let alone your vajra power. The musha sword method, which relies on power and speed, was particularly weak in this aspect.　In this kind of situation, exquisite techniques are the key to success.

敵騎がそれを甲鉄の下に蓄えて俺を待っているならば、間違っても迂闊な進退はできなかった。　無思慮に斬り込みなどした途端、切り返しの一太刀を食って血反吐を吐く。
If the enemy craft was waiting for me with it under its armor, I couldn't make a careless move.　As soon as I thoughtlessly slashed into it, I was hit by a return cut and coughed up blood.

我方の打つ出端を制するか――打ち込ませておいて受け流し、体勢の崩れたところを存分に斬り下げるか。　いずれにせよ、勝負はその一合で終わるだろう。
Either he would control the edge of our attack, or he would let us strike and then catch us and cut us down when we were out of position.　Either way, the game would end with that one battle.

こちらも術を仕込んで臨まねばならない。
We must also prepare our techniques.

My adversary was steadfast.　The offensive energy I unleashed was swept away by the willow wind.

つまりは騙されなかったという事。　今、敵騎が俺の露骨な攻勢を勝機と取り、先んじて打ち倒してくれようと襲い来たならば、満を持しての返しの技で一刀のもとに敵の戦闘力を剥奪できた。
In other words, I was not fooled.　Now, if the enemy craft had taken my blatant offensive as an opportunity to strike first, I could have stripped them of their fighting power with a single sword, using a technique of return that I was fully prepared for.

また、こちらに打ち込ませてから切り返す腹積もりであったとしても、案に相違して待てど暮らせど打ち掛かって来ないこちらの様子に、動揺を生じせしめる事ができた筈だった。
And even if he had planned to let me hit him and then cut him back, he could have been upset that I hadn't waited long enough to hit him.

然りながら敵騎は全くの無反応。　姿勢は揺らがず、剣気も粛然と保たれている。
However, the enemy craft was completely unresponsive.　His posture is unwavering, and his swordsmanship is solemnly maintained.

誘いの術を完全に看破されたのだ。
He had been completely blinded by the luring technique.

（不味いな）
That's not good.

技の失敗のみではなく、それが敵に与えた影響まで慮って、俺は密やかな舌打ちを禁じ得なかった。　今ので、敵は察した筈だ……こちらにも術を用いる用意があるという事実を。
It's not only the failure of the technique, but also the effect it had on the enemy that I couldn't help but secretly click my tongue.　It's a great way to make sure you're getting the most out of your time and money.

益々慎重になり、技は深く巧妙なるを期すだろう。　難敵が余計に難敵と化す。
He will become more and more cautious, and his techniques will become deeper and more skillful.　A difficult enemy will become even more difficult.

下手に仕掛けず、凝と構え続け、敵手の焦燥を待つべきだったか……？　　そう思っても、今となっては詮ない。
Should I have continued to hold my ground and waited for my adversary's impatience? ......　　I'm not sure what to make of this.

挫けている場合ではなかった。　敵は慎重に動くであろうが、それは時間を掛けるという事と必ずしも同義ではないのだ。
This was no time to be discouraged.　The enemy would move cautiously, but that was not necessarily synonymous with taking their time.

策を決すれば、この刹那にも仕掛けて来る。　心気を迷妄させていては対応できない。小さな失敗などさっさと忘れるべきだった。
If he decides on a plan, he will set it in motion in this moment.　If I let my mind wander, I would not be able to deal with it. I should have quickly forgotten my small mistakes.

敵は来る――――　来るだろう。
The enemy will come: ---- will come.

今の音なき攻防で勝負の天秤がやや己の側に傾いたと見たなら、その機を捨て去る筈はない。　天秤が再び平衡に戻るまで――俺が心身を立て直し再び術策を講ずるまで、待ってやる義理などないのだ。
If you see that the balance of the game is slightly tilted in your favor by this soundless attack, you will not abandon the opportunity.　There's no reason to wait until the scales are back in equilibrium - until I've regained control of my body and soul and am ready to devise a new strategy.

ましてこのように、立合の最中――全身の神経感覚を過敏にしている時であれば、その圧迫感たるや途轍もない。　舌の表裏が忽ち干上がり、唇が戦慄いた。

このまま心身を消耗し、足腰を萎えさせるか。　あるいは破れかぶれに攻め掛かるか。　　どちらに陥るにせよ、俺の勝ち目はない。
Will he continue to wear out his body and mind, and let his legs and feet wilt?　Or, I could go on a desperate offensive.　　Either way, there was no way I could win.
